Console output now writes to ColorDTest.txt and can be found at /home/pi/Chromostat/ColorDTest.txt

To change output to a file, press o
To return to this screen press h
To set gain value press g
To run color sensor press r
To run color sensor in manual mode press m
To reset file output, type reset
To view current settings, press v
To reset all settings, type resetAll
To set remove all unwanted lines from file, press c
To toggle light press l
To compete strains, type compete
